# <a name="office-365-operated-by-21vianet"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-104">由世纪互联运营的 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-104">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-p102">由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 旨在满足中国用户对安全可靠的可扩展云服务的需求。此服务由 Microsoft 授权给世纪互联使用的技术提供支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-p102">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet is designed to meet the needs for secure, reliable, and scalable cloud services in China. This service is powered by technology that Microsoft has licensed to 21Vianet.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="08320-107">由 Office 365 的世纪互联版本运营的 Office 365 专为中国而设计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-107">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-108">Microsoft 本身并不运营此服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-108">Microsoft does not operate the service itself.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-109">世纪互联负责运营、提供和管理此服务的交付。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-109">21Vianet operates, provides, and manages delivery of the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-110">世纪互联是中国最大的运营商中立 Internet 数据中心服务提供商，提供托管、托管网络服务及云计算基础结构服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-110">21Vianet is the largest carrier-neutral internet data center services provider in China, providing hosting, managed network services, and cloud computing infrastructure services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-111">通过授权的 Microsoft 技术，世纪互联运营本地 Office 365 数据中心，让用户能够使用 Office 365 服务，同时将数据保留在中国。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-111">By licensing Microsoft technologies, 21Vianet operates local Office 365 datacenters to provide the ability to use Office 365 services while keeping data within China.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-112">世纪互联还提供[订阅、计费服务和支持](https://docs.microsoft.com/Office365/Admin/contact-support-for-business-products?view=o365-21vianet&tabs=phone)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-112">21Vianet also provides [subscription and billing services, as well as support](https://docs.microsoft.com/Office365/Admin/contact-support-for-business-products?view=o365-21vianet&tabs=phone).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="08320-113">这些服务受到中国法律的制约。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-113">These services are subject to Chinese laws.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-p104">鉴于中国服务的独特性（由来自中国境内的数据中心合作伙伴运营），还有一些功能尚未启用。随着时间的推移，客户将能使用功能越来越完整的服务。有关功能差异，请参阅服务说明脚注。有关功能差异的简要概述，请参阅[了解由世纪互联运营的 Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-p104">Due to the unique nature of the China services—operated by a partner from datacenters inside China—there are some features that have not yet been enabled. Customers will see the services come closer to full feature parity over time. See the service description footnotes for differences. For a higher-level overview of differences, see [Learn about Office 365 operated by 21Vianet](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china).</span></span>

## <a name="service-availability-within-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-118">每个计划中的服务可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-118">Service availability within each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-p105">由世纪互联运营的每个 Office 365 计划都包括许多单个服务，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。下表显示了每个 Office 365 计划中可用的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-p105">Each Office 365 plan operated by 21Vianet includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online. The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="08320-121">由 Office 365 的世纪互联版本运营的 Office 365 专为中国而设计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-121">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-226"><sup>1</sup>包括 Office 365 管理、Office 365 套件应用程序、用户帐户管理、域、服务运行状况和连续性、报告、服务更新、帮助和培训、网络等功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-226"><sup>1</sup> Includes features such as Office 365 administration, Office 365 suite apps, user account management, domains, service health and continuity, reporting, service updates, help and training, networking, and so on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-227">有关详细信息，请参阅[平台功能](office-365-operated-by-21vianet.md#platform-features)表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-227">For more information, see the [Platform features](office-365-operated-by-21vianet.md#platform-features) table.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-228"><sup>2</sup>虽然 Project Online 不包括在内，但可以作为单独的附加服务进行购买，也可以免费添加到 Office 365 A1 计划中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-228"><sup>2</sup> Project Online is not included, but can be purchased as a separate add-on service or added for free to the Office 365 A1 plan.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-229"><sup>3</sup>可免费使用 Visio 网页版的浏览功能（查看功能）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-229"><sup>3</sup> Visio for the web consumption (view capability) is available for free.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-230">必须有许可证，才能使用 Visio 网页版的创建和编辑功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-230">Visio for the web create and edit capabilities require a license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-231">有关 Visio 网页版的详细信息，请参阅 [Visio 网页版服务说明](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-231">For more information about Visio for the web, see the [Visio for the web service description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span></span>

## <a name="system-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-234">系统要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-234">System requirements</span></span>

## <a name="security-amp-compliance-center-availability-in-office-365-operated-by-21vianet"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-236">安全与合规中心在由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 中的可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-236">Security &amp; Compliance Center availability in Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-237">由世纪互联运营的任何 Office 365 计划都不提供 Office 365 安全与合规中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-237">The Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center is not available in any plans for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-1146"><sup>1</sup>由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 和 Office 365 不会为不受其制造商支持的任何操作系统提供支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1146"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 and Office 365 operated by 21Vianet do not provide support for any operating system that is not supported by its manufacturer.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1147"><sup>2</sup>在由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 企业 F3 中，office 365 视频仅限于查看（无发布或共享）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1147"><sup>2</sup> In Office 365 Enterprise F3 operated by 21Vianet, Office 365 video is limited to viewing only (no publishing or sharing).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1148"><sup>3</sup>如果要将目录同步与本地 Active Directory 结合使用，必须使用本地 Active Directory（而不是 Office 365 门户），或使用 Windows PowerShell 的 Azure Active Directory 模块删除帐户或更改密码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1148"><sup>3</sup> If you are using directory synchronization with a local Active Directory, you must delete accounts or change passwords by using the local Active Directory, rather than the Office 365 portal or by using the Azure Active Directory module for Windows PowerShell.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1149"><sup>4</sup>在由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 中尚不可用，但即将可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1149"><sup>4</sup> Not yet available in Office 365 operated by 21Vianet, but coming soon.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1150"><sup>5</sup>Office 365 只能有一个公共网站，除非已升级旧版 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1150"><sup>5</sup> You can have only one public website with Office 365 unless you've upgraded from an earlier version of Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1151">在这种情况下，你具有两个公共网站，但只能使用自定义域名托管其中一个公共网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1151">In that case, you have two public websites, but only one of them can be hosted with a custom domain name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1152">若要详细了解如何处理商业版订阅的两个网站，请参阅[处理两个 Office 365 公共网站](https://support.office.com/article/a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1152">For more information about working with the two websites for business subscriptions, see [Work with your two Office 365 public websites](https://support.office.com/article/a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1153">如果有其他订阅，请参阅 [Office 365 公共网站帮助](https://support.office.com/article/a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5)，详细了解公共网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1153">If you have a different subscription, learn more about public websites at [public website help for Office 365](https://support.office.com/article/a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1154"><sup>6</sup>减少按费用折扣购买的席位可能会导致提前终止费用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1154"><sup>6</sup> Reducing seats that were purchased with a term discount may be subject to an early termination fee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1155">这不适用于按月支付的订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1155">This is not applicable for subscriptions paid on a monthly basis.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1156"><sup>7</sup>Office 365 教育版计划不支持通过 Microsoft 365 管理中心更改许可证席位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1156"><sup>7</sup> Office 365 Education plans do not support license seat changes from the Microsoft 365 admin center.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1157"><sup>8</sup>特定地理位置的客户暂无法使用 Microsoft Sway。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1157"><sup>8</sup> Microsoft Sway is not currently available for customers in certain geographies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1158">某些自 2015 年 8 月起市场中不再提供的旧版 Office 365 可能也无法使用 Microsoft Sway。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1158">Some legacy Office 365 plans that are no longer in market as of August 2015 may also not have access to Microsoft Sway.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1159"><sup>9</sup>要了解由世纪互联运营的 Office 365，请在[此处](https://www.21vbluecloud.com/office365/O365-SLA/)查看服务级别协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1159"><sup>9</sup> For Office 365 operated by 21Vianet, see the Service Level Agreement [here](https://www.21vbluecloud.com/office365/O365-SLA/).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1160"><sup>10</sup>了解由世纪互联运营的 Office 365，请查看世纪互联的 [Office 365 联机服务标准协议](https://www.21vbluecloud.com/office365/O365-AgreeWebDir/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1160"><sup>10</sup> For Office 365 operated by 21Vianet, see 21Vianet's [Online Services Standard Agreement for Office 365](https://www.21vbluecloud.com/office365/O365-AgreeWebDir/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-1161"><sup>11</sup>中国互联网合规性策略要求你具备公共网站的 Internet 内容提供商 (ICP) 编号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1161"><sup>11</sup> China internet compliance policy requires that you get an Internet Content Provider (ICP) number for a public website.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1162">有关详细信息，请参阅相应的 ICP 主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1162">For more information, see the corresponding ICP topic.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1163"><sup>12</sup>某些内容可能不适用于由世纪互联运营的 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1163"><sup>12</sup> Some content may not apply to Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1164"><sup>13</sup>体验的质量降低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1164"><sup>13</sup> Diminished experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1165">如果组织依赖 Internet Explorer 8 或 Internet Explorer 9 访问旧版 Web 应用和服务，不妨考虑升级到 Internet Explorer 11，并评估 Internet Explorer 11 企业模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1165">If your organization is dependent upon Internet Explorer 8 or Internet Explorer 9 to access older web apps and services, you may want to consider upgrading to Internet Explorer 11 and evaluating Enterprise Mode for Internet Explorer 11.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1166">此更新有助于改善与旧版 Web 应用的向后兼容性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1166">This update helps provide better backward compatibility for legacy web apps.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1167"><sup>14</sup>在 Outlook Mobile （IOS 和 Android）中目前不支持多重身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1167"><sup>14</sup> Multi-factor authentication is not currently supported in Outlook mobile (iOS and Android).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-1168"><sup>15</sup>世纪互联提供 OneNote 课堂笔记本，但 OneNote 课堂笔记本工具栏不可用于 Windows 10 应用、iPad 和 OneNote 网页版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1168"><sup>15</sup> OneNote Class Notebook is available via 21Vianet, but the OneNote Class Notebook toolbar is not available for Windows 10 apps, iPad, or OneNote for the web.</span></span>

## <a name="office-for-the-web-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-1770">Office 网页版功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1770">Office for the web features</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1771">由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 版本专为中国而设计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1771">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-1772">下表提供了一些链接，可通过它们查看 Office 网页版功能与功能丰富的 Microsoft Office 桌面应用之间的比较结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1772">The following table provides links to comparisons of Office for the web feature capabilities to feature-rich Microsoft Office desktop apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-1773">通过比较结果可了解到 Office 网页版中提供了哪些功能，然后选择功能名称，查看关于其工作原理的简短说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1773">Use the comparisons to discover what features are available in Office for the web, and then select the feature name to read a brief description about how that feature works.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="08320-p122">仅选择了数量有限的 Office 功能来代表 Office 桌面套件的高级功能。此比较表并未列出全部 Microsoft Office 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-p122">A limited selection of Office features has been chosen to represent the advanced capabilities of the Office desktop suite. The comparison tables are not a comprehensive list of Microsoft Office features.</span></span>

> - <span data-ttu-id="08320-1777">如果 Microsoft Office Web Apps Server 2013 本地客户已购买 Office 桌面套件许可证（例如 Office Professional Plus、Office Standard 或 Office 365 专业增强版许可证），则可获得 Office 网页版编辑许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1777">Microsoft Office Web Apps Server 2013 on-premises customers get an Office for the web editing license if they have purchased an Office desktop suite license (such as Office Professional Plus, Office Standard, or an Office 365 ProPlus license).</span></span>

## <a name="exchange-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-1793">Exchange Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1793">Exchange Online features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-1794">下表列出了由世纪互联计划运营的 Office 365 中提供的 Exchange Online 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-1794">The following table lists the Exchange Online services that are available in Office 365 operated by 21Vianet plans.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-2592"><sup>1</sup>某些第三方 Web 部件和外接程序可能不可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2592"><sup>1</sup> Some third-party web parts and add-ins may not be available.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2593"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是一款本地服务器，必须进行单独购买和管理，才能启用支持的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2593"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2594"><sup>3</sup>邮件流规则（也称为传输规则）由灵活条件构成，可方便你根据条件定义条件、异常和要采取的措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2594"><sup>3</sup> Mail flow rules (also known as transport rules) are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions, exceptions and actions to take based on the criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2595">Exchange Online 与 Microsoft Exchange Server 之间的可用条件、例外和操作有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2595">The available conditions, exceptions, and actions differ between Exchange Online and Microsoft Exchange Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2596">有关详细信息，请参阅各产品的相应主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2596">For more information, see the corresponding topics for each product.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2597"><sup>4</sup>只能通过直接访问 Exchange 管理中心 (EAC) 管理界面来访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2597"><sup>4</sup> Only accessible via direct access to the Exchange admin center (EAC) management interface.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2598"><sup>5</sup>Exchange Server 2013 仅使用 Microsoft 反恶意软件引擎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2598"><sup>5</sup> Exchange Server 2013 uses only the Microsoft anti-malware engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2599">Exchange Online 使用多种反恶意软件引擎扫描入站、出站和内部邮件中是否包含恶意软件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2599">Exchange Online uses multiple anti-malware engines to scan inbound, outbound, and internal messages for malware.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2600"><sup>6</sup>可以为需要非活动邮箱功能的每个邮箱单独购买 EOA 订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2600"><sup>6</sup> An EOA subscription can be purchased separately for each mailbox that requires the inactive mailbox feature.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2601"><sup>7</sup>对于电子数据展示，你需要对本地和云单独进行查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2601"><sup>7</sup> For eDiscovery, you need a separate query for on-premises vs. cloud.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2602"><sup>8</sup>支持 POP，但不支持 IMAP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2602"><sup>8</sup> POP is supported, but IMAP is not.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2603"><sup>9</sup>Office 365 商业协作版和商业高级版不提供利用本地服务器的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2603"><sup>9</sup> Office 365 Business Essentials and Business Premium do not provide access rights for utilization with on-premises servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2604">为了兼容，客户必须购买或先前购买了相应的 CAL 或升级至企业版 SKU，后者提供这些访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2604">To be compliant, customer must purchase or have previously purchased the appropriate CALs or upgrade to an Enterprise SKU, which provides these access rights.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-2725"><sup>1</sup> 邮件用户被定义为"邮箱"，并且可以在 Exchange 管理中心 (EAC) 中与外部邮件联系人一起进行添加、删除或直接管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2725"><sup>1</sup> Mail users are defined as "Mailboxes," and, along with external mail contacts, can be added, removed, and otherwise managed directly in the Exchange admin center (EAC).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2726"><sup>2</sup>有 RBAC 自定义项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2726"><sup>2</sup> No RBAC customization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2727">只有管理员角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2727">Admin roles only.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2728"><sup>3</sup>可在 EAC 中查看托管域和编辑域类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2728"><sup>3</sup> Managed domains can be viewed and domain types can be edited in the EAC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2729">其他所有的域管理操作必须在 Microsoft 365 管理中心进行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2729">All other domain management must be done in the Microsoft 365 admin center.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2730"><sup>4</sup>有关 EOP 中的邮件流（也称为传输规则），请参阅 [Exchange Online 保护中的邮件流规则（传输规则）](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2730"><sup>4</sup> Mail flow rules (also known as transport rules) in EOP are described in [Mail flow rules (transport rules) in Exchange Online Protection](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2731">EOP 与 Exchange Online 之间的可用邮件流规则条件、例外和操作有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2731">The available mail flow rule conditions, exceptions, and actions differ slightly between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2732">有关这些区别，请参阅 [Exchange Online 中的邮件流规则条件和异常（谓词）](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions)和 [Exchange Online 中的邮件流规则](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2732">These differences are noted in [Mail flow rule conditions and exceptions (predicates) in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions) and [Mail flow rule actions in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2733"><sup>5</sup>EOP 审核报告是不包括邮箱信息的 Exchange Online 审核报告的子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2733"><sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2734"><sup>5</sup>EOP 审核报告是不包括邮箱信息的 Exchange Online 审核报告的子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2734"><sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2735"><sup>6</sup>默认内容筛选器操作会将垃圾邮件移动到收件人的“垃圾邮件”文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2735"><sup>6</sup> The default content filter action is to move spam messages to the recipients' Junk Email folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2736">要将此筛选器与本地 Exchange 邮箱结合使用，还需要在本地 Exchange 组织上配置两条传输规则，用于检测 EOP 添加的垃圾邮件头。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2736">For this to work with on-premises Exchange mailboxes, you also need to configure two transport rules in your on-premises Exchange organization to detect spam headers added by EOP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2737">有关详细信息，请参阅 [确保垃圾邮件已路由到每个用户的"垃圾邮件"文件夹](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2737">For more information, see [Ensure that spam is routed to each user's Junk Email folder](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2738"><sup>7</sup>此功能适用于将通过 EOP 筛选其邮箱的 Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) 客户，并且很快将提供给 Exchange Online 客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2738"><sup>7</sup> This feature is available to Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) customers whose mailboxes are being filtered by EOP, and will soon be available to Exchange Online customers.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2739"><sup>8</sup>EOP 报告是不包括邮箱信息的 Exchange Online 报告的子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2739"><sup>8</sup> EOP reports are a subset of Exchange Online reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2740"><sup>9</sup>包括 DLP 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2740"><sup>9</sup> Includes DLP reports.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2741"><sup>10</sup>扫描入站和出站邮件，但不扫描从组织中的发件人发送给组织中的收件人的内部邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2741"><sup>10</sup> Scans inbound and outbound messages, but does not scan internal messages sent from a sender in your organization to a recipient in your organization.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2742"><sup>11</sup>EOP 和 Exchange Online 的可用谓词和操作不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2742"><sup>11</sup> The available predicates and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2743"><sup>12</sup>混合安装程序不能通过混合向导使用，但是，如果你拥有 Exchange SP1，则可以手动进行设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2743"><sup>12</sup> Hybrid setup is not available through Hybrid Wizard, but can be set up manually if you have Exchange SP1.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-2744"><sup>13</sup>当前 Office 365 邮件加密 (OME) 功能是由当前的信息权限管理 (IRM) 和之前的 OME 解决方案发展而来的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2744"><sup>13</sup> The current Office 365 Message Encryption (OME) capabilities are an evolution of the current Information Rights Management (IRM) and previous OME solutions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2745">有关 OME 的详细信息，请参阅 [Office 365 邮件加密常见问题解答](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/compliance/ome-faq)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2745">For more information about OME, see [Office 365 Message Encryption FAQ](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/compliance/ome-faq).</span></span>

## <a name="exchange-online-archiving-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-2746">Exchange Online Archiving 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2746">Exchange Online Archiving features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-2747">可通过以下计划使用 Exchange Online Archiving。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2747">Exchange Online Archiving is available through the following plans.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2748">由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 版本专为中国而设计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2748">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="08320-2749">**计划**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2749">**Plan**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="08320-2750">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2750">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="08320-2751">**适于由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 的 Exchange Online Archiving for Exchange Server**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2751">**Exchange Online Archiving for Exchange Server for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="08320-2752">基于云的存档，适用于在 Exchange Server 2013 或 Exchange 2010（SP2 或更高版本）中拥有主邮箱的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2752">Cloud-based archive for users with primary mailboxes in Exchange Server 2013 or Exchange 2010 (SP2 or later).</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="08320-p137">如果想要将基于云的存档添加到位于本地 Exchange 服务器上的主邮箱，则需要配置混合部署。有关混合部署的详细信息，请参阅 [Exchange Server 混合部署](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/exchange-hybrid)。  </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-p137">If you want to add a cloud-based archive to a primary mailbox that's located on an on-premises Exchange server, you need to configure a hybrid deployment. For more information about hybrid deployments see [Exchange Server Hybrid Deployments](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/exchange-hybrid).</span></span>|

<span data-ttu-id="08320-2820"><sup>2</sup>就地存档仅可用于为单个用户存档邮件或为应用了许可证的实体存档邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2820"><sup>2</sup> In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity for which a license has been applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2821">禁止使用就地存档作为存储多位用户或实体的邮件的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2821">Using an In-Place Archive as a means to store mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-2822">例如，IT 管理员无法创建共享邮箱且无法使用户复制（通过“抄送”/“密件抄送”字段或邮件流规则）共享邮箱来显式存档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2822">For example, IT administrators can't create shared mailboxes and have users copy (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a mail flow rule) a shared mailbox for the explicit purpose of archiving.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-2824"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是一款本地服务器，必须进行单独购买和管理，才能启用支持的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2824"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="08320-2825"><sup>5</sup>将邮箱置于就地保留或诉讼保留时，主邮箱和存档邮箱都会被置于相应的保留。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-2825"><sup>5</sup> When you put a mailbox on In-Place Hold or Litigation Hold, the hold is placed on both the primary and the archive mailbox.</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-4720"><sup>7</sup>经过身份验证的 SharePoint Online 用户可以使用分面导航访问专用网站集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4720"><sup>7</sup> Authenticated SharePoint Online users can access private site collections with faceted navigation.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-4721"><sup>8</sup>Kiosk 用户无法使用动态磁贴创建 Office 文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4721"><sup>8</sup> Kiosk users cannot create Office documents using live tiles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-4722">要创建文档，Kiosk 用户必须选择“**新建**”，然后从“**创建新文件**”菜单选择一种文件类型（Word 文档、Excel 工作簿、PowerPoint 演示文稿、OneNote 笔记本或 Excel 调查），通过 SharePoint Online 网站进行创建。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4722">To create a document, kiosk users must do so from a SharePoint Online site by selecting **New** and then selecting a file type - Word document, Excel workbook, PowerPoint presentation, OneNote notebook, or Excel survey - from the **Create a new file** menu.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-4723"><sup>9</sup>你所在的国家/地区可能会阻止某些提供商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4723"><sup>9</sup> Some providers may be blocked in your country/region.</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-4727"><sup>11</sup>Kiosk 帐户具有受限的 OneDrive for Business 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4727"><sup>11</sup> Kiosk accounts have limited OneDrive for Business functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-4728">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4728">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-4729">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB or 5 TB of online storage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4729">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB or 5 TB of online storage.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="08320-4730"><sup>12</sup>可在任何移动浏览器中查看文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4730"><sup>12</sup> You can view documents in any Mobile browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-4731">您需要安装 Office Mobile 应用来编辑文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4731">You need to install the Office Mobile app to edit documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-4732">Office Mobile is currently available for Windows phones and tablets, Android phones and tablets, iPhone, and iPad.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4732">Office Mobile is currently available for Windows phones and tablets, Android phones and tablets, iPhone, and iPad.</span></span>

## <a name="skype-for-business-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-4738">Skype for Business Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4738">Skype for Business Online features</span></span>

> - <span data-ttu-id="08320-4740">此表指明了各个 Office 365 产品可用的客户端和服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4740">This table indicates client and service availability across Office 365 options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="08320-4741">若要比较各种 Skype for Business 桌面客户端、Web 客户端和移动客户端的各项功能，请参阅[桌面客户端比较表](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables)和[移动客户端比较表](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-mobile-client-comparison-tables)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-4741">If you want to compare individual features among the various Skype for Business desktop clients, web clients, and mobile clients, see [Desktop client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables) and [Mobile Client Comparison Tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-mobile-client-comparison-tables).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="08320-5744">由 Office 365 的世纪互联版本运营的 Office 365 专为中国而设计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-5744">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="08320-p152">Skype for Business Online 独立计划 2 的许可用户将获得 Skype for Business 基本客户端，而不是完整的 Skype for Business 客户端。如果您想让用户拥有 Skype for Business 客户端，您需要将其升级到包括它的许可证，例如，基于企业的许可证。若要向您的用户部署 Skype for Business 客户端，请参阅[部署 Office 365 中的 Skype for Business 客户端](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-skype-for-business-online/deploy-the-skype-for-business-client-in-office-365)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-p152">Skype for Business Online Standalone Plan 2 licensed users will get the Skype for Business Basic client, not the full Skype for Business client. If you want users to have the Skype for Business client, you will need to upgrade them to a license that includes it, such as an Enterprise-based license. To deploy the Skype for Business client to your users, see [Deploy the Skype for Business client in Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-skype-for-business-online/deploy-the-skype-for-business-client-in-office-365).</span></span>

## <a name="follow-on-wechat"></a><span data-ttu-id="08320-6627">在 WeChat 上关注此服务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-6627">Follow on WeChat</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="08320-6628">扫描此 QR 码在 WeChat 上关注这项服务，获取由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 的最新动态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08320-6628">Scan this QR code to follow discussions on WeChat and get the latest updates for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span>

![WeChat 的 QR 代码](../media/8f6064e6-ccf3-4050-97e3-619058b3c806.jpg)
